вњ¦ The AuthApiTest is failing with a BindingResolutionException for hash because it currently extends PHPUnit\Framework\TestCase. It
  needs a booted Laravel application to run Eloquent factories, hashing functions like bcrypt(), and HTTP assertions like
  $this->postJson().

  My proposed strategy is to change AuthApiTest to extend the application's base Tests\TestCase class instead of PHPUnit's default
  TestCase.

  Does this approach sound good to you? Once you confirm, I'll draft the plan.
